    <aside id="interscroller_ad" class="interscroller_ad visible-xs center mobile-interscroller " style="width:300px"></aside>
    <script>
        var mps = mps || {};
        mps._queue = mps._queue || {};
        mps._queue.gptloaded = mps._queue.gptloaded || [];
        mps._queue.adload = mps._queue.adload || [];

        mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
            if (mps.getResponsiveSet() =='0') { //MOBILE
                mps.insertAd('#interscroller_ad','interscroller');
            }
        });
        mps._queue.adload.push(function(eo) {
            if (eo._mps._slot === 'interscroller' && eo.isEmpty) {
                document.querySelector('.mobile-interscroller').classList.add('isEmpty');
            }
        });
    </script>

When he meets Peter Parker, he soon realizes that there are many others who share his special, high-flying talents. <section id="audience_reviews" class="panel panel-rt panel-box" data-qa="audience-reviews">
    <h2 class="panel-heading">Audience Reviews for <em>Spider-Man: Into the Spider-Verse</em></h2>
    
        
        <div class="sr-only js-clamp-live-region" aria-live="polite"></div>
        <ul class="mop-audience-reviews__reviews-wrap clearfix">
            
            
            
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Oct 19, 2020</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Who would think an animated Spiderman could outshine it&#39;s bigger budgeted counterparts.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/901357030">
                            
                                <img class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-avatar" src="https://graph.facebook.com/v3.3/1364461619/picture"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/901357030">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Mark B</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">May 07, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">So when I heard Sony was doing an animated Spider-Man, good lord this is about a million miles from where I thought they would be.  By that I mean good, like, really good.  Like, maybe the best Spider-Man movie ever good?  Is that even possible?  It&#39;s weird because it even does things that were terrible mistakes in other movies and does them here in a way that works out with artistic brilliance.  For example, when Ang Lee did stylized comic panels in Hulk, it was confusing and weird.  When this movie does it, it adds to the energy and atmosphere of the film without ever interrupting the flow of the action.  How?  How did they do that?  Maybe because this whole movie is basically a comic book.  The characters look more like comic books than ever, and even the different Spider-Men have different art styles to them, and did I mention the &quot;bing&quot; and &quot;pow&quot; and &quot;bagel&quot; text sound effects and even thought bubbles that will appear over their heads?  This movie just oozes so much style.  And we get so many cool Spider-Men, and so many cool villains, and somehow it never feels crowded like it did in Spider-Man 3 or X3.  Again, mistakes in the past but here it works.  What the hell!  And it does all of this without missing it&#39;s emotional core.  Actually my favorite moment in the movie isn&#39;t a big action sequence, it&#39;s a small moment of all the Spider-Men sharing their experiences of loss, and experience they can all only share with each other.  It&#39;s surprisingly powerful considering one of the characters involved is a talking pig.  Really if I had a critique, it would be wanting a few more moments like this.  Also probably more of other Spider-Men, because really this story is Miles, Peter, and Gwen&#39;s story and the other three are more or less background.  I would have liked it to be more even, but that might have pushed the magic formula.  Honestly I shouldn&#39;t be complaining because that this works at all is amazing  That it&#39;s this damn good is a godamn miracle.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/901376268">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/901376268">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Michael M</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Mar 31, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Phil Lord continues to hit, particularly on the animated front. This film is wonderfully original, which is important after the number of Spider-Man movies I&#39;ve seen in my lifetime, it&#39;s also beautifully animated and just as heartfelt as it is funny. The actual plot is a bit lacking, and when you&#39;re dealing with a story about multiple dimensions there&#39;s bound to be some frustrating plot holes and questions, but the other aspects of this film are so great that they nearly completely cover up this film&#39;s flaws.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/905108980">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/905108980">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Sanjay R</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Mar 14, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">A joyously weird ride. As funny and sweet as the movie is, the real triumph is the animation which is unlike anything I&#39;ve ever seen.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/790680964">
                            
                                <img class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-avatar" src="https://graph.facebook.com/v3.3/20312798/picture"></span>
